    <li> I&#x27;ve had this set for two years now.  I&#x27;ve recharged the battery twice.  Great product if your unsightly ear and nose hair needs professional removal.  the other attachments work well too.</li>
    <li> When I saw the price (~$188), I laughed.  I&#x27;ve owned this unit for years ... it&#x27;s not worth $188.  The listed price has to be a mistake.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Currently looking for a similar trimmer with more attachments.</li>
    <li> the shaver itself seems good but charger stopped working in first few days...&lt;br /&gt;I sent it outside US so could not get it replaced under warranty as well... bad experience.</li>

    <li> This is an inexpensive groomer that has quite a few features.  The only thing I don&#x27;t like is that when you are charging it, you have no idea if it is fully charged or not.  A blinking light or some indication that it is fully charged would be nice.  Adjustments work well, and it gives a clean finish to your shave.</li>
    <li> It works good, It has all functionality one may need. And  for information. Philips uses the same materials as for expensive models so the quality is guaranteed.</li>
    <li> Excellent trimmer, charges just fine, with easy cleanup.</li>
    <li> I&#x27;ve never had a beard trimmer before (nor a beard). These trimmers make it pretty easy to maintain it at just the length that I like. I got it mainly for the beard trimmer attachment. The nose hair, precision trimmer, and foil shaver attachments work well too. The full length trimmer works pretty well, but even the longest length is practically a buzz cut, I wish the lengths extended to even longer. Overall it&#x27;s great, and it&#x27;s convenient that it has a rechargeable battery in it. I&#x27;m not enamored by it, but I like it :)</li>
    <li> I have the Philips Norelco G370 All-in-1 Grooming System, had it less than a year. The battery is the main issue...it will not stay charged more than one day - even when not used.  Other trimmer parts seem to work pretty well...except the rotary hair/nose hair clipper pulls (yikes!) out about as many hairs as it cuts. The clippers, are supposed to be washable, rust pretty quickly if you don&#x27;t get ALL the water out. It helps to add a very light amount of clipper oil to keep these running smoothly.&lt;br /&gt;Main problem is that Phillips Norelco wants me to pay shipping and insurance so they can evaluate my G370...must have receipt (who keeps these?), etc. and this is just to decide if they&#x27;ll honor their 2 year warranty. By the time I pay for shipping, and the time it takes to do all this, I may as well get a different clipper.&lt;br /&gt;All for the lack of a decent battery...you should be ashamed Phillips Norelco!</li>
    <li> Ive had this trimmer for about 6 months now. I mainly use it to cut my hair and its done a pretty good job.&lt;br /&gt;But here are a couple of problems with this trimmer.&lt;br /&gt;The first has to do wit the beard trimming attachment. The first time i used it, it cut me under my chin and it was so painful!!! Which made me not use it for a couple of weeks and when i did use it again it did the exact same thing!!! Hopefully ive learned my lesson.&lt;br /&gt;The second and WORST problem it has, is that you cant use it and charge it at the same time.&lt;br /&gt;I knew you couldnt when i bought it cause i had read it in the reviews. But i didnt think it was going to be so inconvenient. I thought to my self \\&quot;oh ill just make sure its always charged\\&quot;.  Easier said than done!&lt;br /&gt;Time and time again it has died in the middle of me cutting my hair. And it wouldnt be so bad if it charged quickly but it doesnt!! An hour long charge only last me about 30 seconds to 1 minute  of usage!! Its insane!!!&lt;br /&gt;So just take my advice and buy a better trimmer because i guarantee you the same things that happened to me will happen to you</li>
    <li> This is the second time I&#x27;ve bought this trimmer, though the first one was gray and had a stand. I now know what I did wrong with the first one and why they did not include the stand this time. DO NOT RECHARGE this device until it needs recharging. I charged it once a year ago when I purchased it and keep a very stylized beard and it&#x27;s still going strong on that one charge. My previous trimmer lasted me a couple of years but that was with me constantly charging it in the stand. I kept the old stand but I don&#x27;t plug it in.</li>
    <li> The razor&#x27;s cutting units were very sharp and got the job done, quick, fast, and in a hurry!!! Would definitely recommended this product to others!</li>

    <li> This is a great device at the price it originally sold for while it was in production, ~15 at triple digit prices it&#x27;s not even in play.</li>
    <li> I love this groomer. I have had it for quite some time now and it&#x27;s still going strong. I use it on myself, my man and now our little one. Much easier to manage than the old standard plug in style. Small, strong, effective and versatile.</li>
    <li> I purchased this item for my grandson.  He liked all of the accessories; however, he hasn&#x27;t actually used it yet so we don&#x27;t know how well it perform.</li>
    <li> Nothing fancy.. just does what its supposed to do.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;I would definitely recommend this product to anyone who doesnt want to shell out much for a trimmer.</li>
    <li> To start, I didnt expect this to be the best device in terms of quality and longevity for $19.00 but it holds its own in terms of bang for the buck. I decided to give it the first couple weeks of home use and then my most recent 10 day vacation of use before writing my review. The G370 does a really good job on daily facial hair maintenance. I used the mini foil shaver, both edge trimmers and the nose/ear hair trimmer. I havent used the 2 hair/head trimmer attachments as I really didnt need to with a 3 week haircut regimen. The mini foil attachment really surprised me, it really got me by during my vacation in the areas I wanted the least amount of hair. It doesnt replace my actual razor at home but sufficed well while out of town for more than a week. The larger of the two edge trimmers I used as a chin and beard groomer for the days I opted for the 5 o&#x27; clock shadow look and the smaller edge trimmer really helps in the fine line areas of trimming as well as touching up around the ears/hairline. I used the nose/ear trimmer a couple times and it works pretty good, well enough I didnt get bothered by nose hairs tickling my nostrils at all, heheh. It holds a charge for a very long time &amp; offers enough power to get the job done in a timely mannor. I went 5 days on a single charge while on vacation and honestly only attached it to the charger to be sure it would have full potential for shaving &amp; trimming, not because it was dieing or running out of charge! All the attchments remove and connect easily and can easily be cleaned form hair debris with the offered cleaning brush. I think some purchasers were using water to rinse thier attachments but I opted not to just to add to the longevity of the metal parts. The only attachment that I used that collected the most hair internally was the foil shaver wich is a double attachment (2 pieces) that allows for easier cleaning. If I never used the trimmer ever again I feel I got my moneys worth out of it already. To end this review, Id like to note that I believe some reviewers leaving negative feedback were expecting the results of a $100+ shaver/trimmer. I went into this purchase expecting a $20 trimmmer and feel I got that and more and will continue to keep this in use on a regular basis along with my regular home shaving items (razors/shaving cream, etc)!iew, Id like to note that I believe some reviewers leaving negative feedback were expecting the results of a $100+ shaver/trimmer. I went into this purchase expecting a $20 trimmmer and feel I got that and more and will continue to keep this in use on a regular basis along with my regular home shaving items (razors/shaving cream, etc)!</li>
    <li> Everything is as advertised. It works great and has a bunch of different settings for length. Great quality for the price.</li>
    <li> I had one like this for over 7 years. the beard trimming attachment broke (not the actual razor), so I thought it was time to get a new one. I bought the exact same model because it has been incredibly durable and the only reason the trimming attachment broke was due to my rough treatment of it. I highly recommend this.</li>
    <li> I got this product for my bf cause he travels a lot and recently lost his personal shaver. He liked it. When I told him it wasn&#x27;t very expensive and asked him how it was? His words were &amp;#34;its really very good for its price. &amp;#34;</li>
    <li> i&#x27;ve basically stopped using blades since i purchased this electric razor. it should pay for itself with what i saved on the blades in no time.</li>
    <li> Small design makes it easy to manoeuvre especially around the ears. One adjustable guide makes it easy to switch to the size you need. However it easily clogs the hair in the guide (not the blade itself!) and you need to remove the guide altogether at least once per session. Takes about 10-12 hours to charge for a use of at least 20-30 minutes. I did not check exactly how long it lasts.&lt;br /&gt;It is recommended to let the charge drain between usage, not kept plugged in continually.&lt;br /&gt;Holds the charge well for now.  Great for the price. Thanks amazon.</li>
    <li> right for the price right for the price right for the price right for the price&lt;br /&gt;not very easy to clean&lt;br /&gt;but cheap, so that is enough</li>
    <li> The trimmer itself works fine. It feels pretty sturdy and seems to run fine. It holds a charge really well, I don&#x27;t have to charge it very often.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;The attachments are sort of cheap and you have to be really careful when you are putting them on the razor. On the &#x27;hair comb&#x27; attachment, the little black plastic piece that locks in a length broke the 5th time I used it. I called Norelco @ 1-800-243-3050 and they sent me a free replacement, which they noted they would only do once. The other ones do the job, but again, they feel sort of cheap.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;If you&#x27;re on a budget, then go ahead and pick this trimmer up, but be really careful with the attachments. But if you have a few extra bucks, I might shop around for a razor that is higher quality and that comes with nicer attachments.</li>
    <li> Good value for the money. This thing comes with a slew of attachments, most of which I don&#x27;t need, but you never know!  This unit charges fast and is extremely light and easy to handle. Highly recommended for home use!&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;My last Conair ($14) groomer lasted 10+ years- let&#x27;s see how this puppy does!</li>
    <li> You get what you pay for.  The clippers are too small for any serious hair cutting.  The razor is only good for detail work like getting a sharp edge on side burns.  Would take for ever to actually do your whole face.  However, it was worth the price for the nose and ear trimmer.  Works great (loud in your ears though).</li>
    <li> As long as you dont expect any use out of the shaver this is a great product.</li>
    <li> This machine have a lot to offer i just need to get use to to hold it in the right angle to not make mistake is good for the price im happy :)</li>
    <li> I purchased this product mainly because I was sold on the versatility. Five different attachments, so no need to buy separate products. But if you are in the market for a multi-use trimmer, I&#x27;d look elsewhere.    First, I had two separate chargers die on me. The first one died after three weeks. A trip to Radio Shack said that a replacement charger would run $30 or more than the cost of a new one. I returned the product and purchase a new G370 thinking maybe I got a black swan. Guess not, because the second charger just died on me after about 6 months.    Charger issues aside, I mainly used the full size trimmer attachment with the adjustable levels and the beard &amp; mustache trimmer. The full size trimmer was good at adjusting my facial hair down to a \\&quot;one\\&quot; or fuller than a five o&#x27;clock shadow but just enough to keep it professional. This was about the only thing the unit was good at. I used the beard and mustache trimmer to keep my sideburns neat when I didn&#x27;t have the two-day growth going. While the G370 did neatly square them off, in my opinion, it didn&#x27;t trim the hair short enough. I tried to finish off my sideburns then with the razor attachment but also that didn&#x27;t get things short enough. I did use the nose hair trimmer four or five times and I&#x27;d say that the G370 did okay in that area.     I never tried to trim my hair with the G370, but it feels flimsy enough where I wouldn&#x27;t trust it to cut hair evenly or professionally. Also, the unit seems to run best on a full charge (obviously) but would quickly die off in terms of effectiveness after one or two uses. If you are thinking of packing it on a business trip greater than five days (i.e. two/three trimmings) then I&#x27;d suggest bringing a charger with you (if it doesn&#x27;t die).     I&#x27;d suggest looking at a few product levels up from the G370 and paying extra to get a more quality trimming unit.</li>
    <li> Cheap and works VERY well. This is the second one I&#x27;ve had. Extremely happy with it.</li>
    <li> This set is all I need. Easy to use and works great. This is a replacement set for the older version of this set...which lasted about seven years of me dropping and using and finally the grooming guard broke. Great set at a great price!</li>
    <li> This is the second Norelco trimmer that I have bought. The first one is about 8 years old and the only reason I had to buy this one is because I dropped it and broke part of it. This works well and has great features. I would definitely recommend.</li>
    <li> This trimmer is very disappointing. According to the description, this trimmer is \\&quot;self-sharpening\\&quot; and has a full two-year warranty.     <li> I received the item as a gift, and I didn&#x27;t already have a trimmer, so I decided to open the package and use it despite the myriad negative reviews. I have an average beard - not too thick, not too thin, but full face coverage. I keep it trimmed under 1 inch almost all the time, and usually much shorter.    Packaging:  The package is a blister pack which encloses the trimmer, attachments, carrying case, the base stand/holder, and a charging adapter. The charging adapter can be attached to the base stand, although it&#x27;s a pretty cheesy design. The packaging is attractive and protective in PET recyclable plastic, and all the necessary operating parts are included.    Design:  The base stand/holder is thin plastic, cheaply made, and barely functional. The attachments are likewise cheap, poorly made plastic with barely functional adjusting mechanism. The trimmer unit has a fixed internal battery which is charged by plugging in a 1.6 volt, 80 mA power supply with positive tip - a small yellow one that is the same size often used to charge mobile phones and bluetooth devices. Previous reviewers are correct in saying that the trimmer cannot be powered directly from a wall outlet. The user can leave it plugged in during operation, but it will not draw wall power in any way (the LED indicator shuts off) when the trimmer switch is on. The trimmer unit seems thus far to be solidly built.    Function:  I gave the item 2 stars because it works for trimming facial hair, but not very well. It cuts slowly and awkwardly even through hair on accessible areas of the face and neck. Attachments are adjustable for various hair lengths, but the user soon discovers that the attachment and adjustment mechanisms are inexact and flimsy.     The trimming process is not a pleasant experience, and the poor design and cheap construction are the reasons why. In my first attempt, the trimming attachment went careening into the nearby toilet. If I keep the item, I anticipate having the experience ofholding the attachments on the trimmer, as previous reviews have commented. The manufacturer provides a 45-day money back guarantee if the product is postmarked within the time period and mailed along with the store receipt. Call 800.243.3050 for authorization. Defective products will be repaired or replaced without charge for a period of two years from date of purchase.    In summary:  Flimsy. Barely functional. Not worth $20, but possibly worth $5-$10. Do not expect this to be a lifelong friend, but it should work for a short period of time or in a pinch. Other brands I have used, including Wahl and even Conair, have worked much better. This should not be considered an indictment of all Philips Norelco products, as I have been satisfied with others. In this case, however, consider paying more for a better product.</li>

    <li> Decided to look for a new beard and mustache trimmer when my trusty old Norelco Maverick TX-450 finally gave up the ghost and just quit running. If this sounds like I&#x27;m slamming the product, I&#x27;m not, as I had owned this basic battery-operated trimmer for over sixteen years - far longer than I ever expected it to last when I first got it. I could have probably fixed it (again) if I disassembled and cleaned it out, but decided to see what might be new on the market. This was primarily used as a mustache trimmer, but after using it for a few years with a handheld comb, was able to do a fair job with my beard.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Was amazed to see how many models were now available, and how many companies were making them. After doing some research (and asking my barber), ended up getting the [[ASIN:B000FED5DU Philips Norelco G370 All-in-1 Grooming System]], and must say that so far this seems to have been a good choice. My barber had suggested that I stay with the more basic (and more economical) trimmers, as most from a particular manufacturer have the same heads as their higher-priced models, and it was the cutting head itself that made a trimmer good or bad. He had suggested that I consider some of the Wahl and Panasonic models, but also had a personal preference for the Philips Norelco products, as they seemed to last... which I had also experienced.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;This trimmer has a great array of attachments, and each of them is quite useful, performing exactly as expected. It has an excellent beard and moustache comb/guide with nine locking length settings, as does the hair clipper comb. The little mini-shaver attachment is good for cleanup, and acts like a miniature micro-screen electric razor. Was cautious about the nose and ear trimmer, but after reading the instruction sheet, found that it was easy to master.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;This model features:&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;* Six attachments that can be rinsed, making it easy to clean&lt;br /&gt;* Nine length settings with the key trimming attachments&lt;br /&gt;* Self-sharpening blades, no oil needed&lt;br /&gt;* Small travel pouch&lt;br /&gt;* Two-year factory warranty&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Took the time to read the instruction sheet that came with this trimmer, which was detailed but easy to understand. The instructions had indicated that the trimmer shouldn&#x27;t be left with the unit charging full-time, which I found to be a nuisance at first. Charged it for the ten hours suggested before using it, and it worked fine, and a charge lasts for weeks. The charging/attachment stand itself looked to be a bit flimsy at first glance, but while handling it when I was setting it up, found that it was sturdier than I had first thought.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Please Note: According to the latest info, this small charging stand no longer comes with the G370 as it did when I first reviewed it in 2009. It no longer appears on the Philips Norelco site as an option, either. Mine was made in China, which made me skeptical at first, but my initial doubts were eased over time, as it has proven to be an excellent trimmer over the long run. I do not know where the current versions are made, but go by the product description if it matters to you.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;This unit, as so many products today, came in one of those irritating theft-deterrent clamshell packages designed for retail stores. This one was more of a nuisance to open than most because it was difficult to see if the contents were going to be damaged when cutting through the plastic with a combination of scissors and a sharp knife. Just be careful when opening it.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Pros:&lt;br /&gt;- Excellent selection of attachments&lt;br /&gt;- Green light on power unit indicates charging&lt;br /&gt;- A single charge lasts for weeks&lt;br /&gt;- Good ergonomics, nice feel to it&lt;br /&gt;- Solid; seems to be built well&lt;br /&gt;- Detailed instruction sheet&lt;br /&gt;- 60-day money-back guarantee, 2-year warranty&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Cons:&lt;br /&gt;- Horrible clamshell package, difficult to open&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Since we all have different things that we look for in trimmerslike this, thought that I might share some of my findings with others here.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Also considered the [[ASIN:B000FED5DK Philips Norelco G380 All-in-1 Grooming System]], but the only difference between this and the Philips Norelco G370 Trimmer was that the G380 came in a gray color and had a travel pouch... which also came with the black G370 trimmer.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Looked at the [[ASIN:B000FEF1V4 Philips Norelco T980 Turbo Vacuum Trimmer]] which was considered for its hair deflector and vacuum, but the price difference was enough to make me go for the more basic G370 trimmer.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;The [[ASIN:B00009RF1E Wahl 9918-617 Groomsman Beard and Mustache Trimmer]] seemed to be a good one, and its ability to operate cordless via battery or plugged into charger sounded good, and it had good reviews. This was a very close second choice.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;The [[ASIN:B000GP5752 Wahl 9877-500 \\&quot;The Goatee\\&quot; Advanced Dual Blade, Rechargeable/Cordless Beard, Goatee &amp; Mustache Trimmer]] had some interesting dual blades, but the Philips Norelco G370 had more attachments, and the model that I looked at made me shy away from this one.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Had also considered the stylish [[ASIN:B000VKV29M Panasonic ER2403K 5 Position Beard/Moustache Trimmer]]. This one features wet or dry trimming, five length adjustments and an excellent price, but since it uses two AAA batteries, decided to rule it out.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;In the end, it was my past experience with the Philips Norelco products that helped make my choice, and I don&#x27;t regret it. If I can get even a fourth of the life of the sixteen years of service that I got from my original Maverick TX-450, then I&#x27;ll be happy.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Updated January 10, 2012:&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Have been using this Philips Norelco G370 trimmer for almost three years since this review was posted on January 24, 2009. Actually wondered how long it would really last when I originally posted it, with most of the concerns being (1) the life of the rechargeable battery, and (2) the sharpness of the blades on the attachments. Had shaved my beard off in 2010, so it became a daily moustache trimmer. Then I grew the beard again a little over a year ago, and it has seen daily use once again.     <li> I purchased the Philips Norelco G370/60 grooming system after going up and down the price points and reviews here at Amazon and in some local stores.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Never having had a hair clipper/beard trimmer before, I had no idea where to start, or which is \\&quot;the one\\&quot;, so decided to try this little guy then go from here if necessary.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;My main objective is to keep a short beard even and clean-looking; secondarily to keep the ear and nose hairs in check and maybe even start learning how to do some hair touch-ups between barbers.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;The instructions are printed on one of those huge newspaper-type sheets and depend hevily on cross-referenced diagrams. After awhile I gave up on that and went by the descriptions on the clamshell container it shipped in. Not going to take any stars for the instructions but they&#x27;re pretty pitiful.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;The basics you need to know are:&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;1. Charge it for 10 hours before using.&lt;br /&gt;2. Use the battery all the way up before recharing to get longest life&lt;br /&gt;3. The silver squarish button on top in front of the power slider is your head-release button. Hold that in and the blade guard and attachments (such as the nose hair trimmer) come off.&lt;br /&gt;4. The beard trimmer and the hair trimmer have a button underneath that allow you to position the trimmer guard closer or further away from the blades. That setting is marked underneath 1 to 9 on the razor and are visible through a little cutout. Also that same guard button is used to take the guards the rest of the way off the razor.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;That&#x27;s really about it. I found that if you use the nose-hair trimmer mostly in an in-out motion instead of side-to-side, you will eliminate the pulling some people have mentioned in their reviews.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Tip: The reviewers that have mentioned that the body of the trimmer is slick and easy to drop are correct. I took two, 2-inch x 1/2\\&quot; pieces of self-adhesive stair tread tape (like you see on skateboards- from any large Home Supply Store), and attached a strip to each side of the trimmer body just behind the finger cut-outs. Now there&#x27;s a good solid grip.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;For the money this little trimmer is really a great value, I actually look forward to using it- it makes a neat job and does not create \\&quot;rows\\&quot; from the trim guards.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;For the closest shave in bare areas, I follow up with my 3-bladed regular \\&quot;wet\\&quot; razor. Really, you couldn&#x27;t tell that this was not done in a professional shop. Very pleased.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;UPDATE December 15, 2012: Still using this on the original battery charge from December 1st and getting good use out of it. How can you beat this for under fourteen bucks shipped with Amazon Prime? :-) I wish someone would have given one to me for Christmas last year!</li>

    <li> I decided to try growing a small beard, so I bought a $10 Wahl beard trimmer. I liked how the beard was looking and decided to upgrade to something rechargeable. I downgraded my Wahl to manscape and got this because it had a lot more features.    I&#x27;ve had this product for 2 months and this is what I can say so far.    Battery - Great life. About 40 minutes of life per 10 hour charge. Not a problem if you can time your days properly. You CANNOT plug the unit in and shave if there is no energy in the battery which is a feature that would have been nice to have.    Trimmer - There are actually two trimmers. One is wider than the other and the smaller trimmer is supposed to be for fine details. The trimmer attachments only clip on to the wider trimmer! I personally use the wide trimmer with the trimmer attachment then pop off the wide trimmer with the attachment and put the thinner attachment on for detail spots (it&#x27;s quicker than taking the trimmer attachment on and off).    The blades seem to be of good quality and claim that they don&#x27;t need oil or sharpening. They are easy on the skin (unlike a previous Remington unit that cut me without attachments).    Trimmer Attachments - There is a hair clipper and a beard trimmer attachment. Again, they attach to the big trimmer only.  I enjoy how the beard trimmer has a tension which hugs your face on the various curves. You can adjust the length easily. People claim that this breaks easily; while the design could have been better, only a great force of pushing the unit to your face will cause it to break. And if it does break, a simple examination of how the attachment works, a paper clip, and super glue will fix it. Again, this product is $16, don&#x27;t expect titanium components. I haven&#x27;t used the hair clippers yet, but i&#x27;m sure the battery will last long enough for a good cut.    The Foil Shaver Attachment - It hurts me and i have to go over a spot several times because it is so small. I just use the smaller trimmer and leaveit or use my other shaver or razor.    Nose/Eyebrow Trimmer - OW! This tends to pull a lot. My $10 Wahl trimmer came with nose trimmer and it worked a lot better.    Stand/Brush - Good. Sleek looking.      You get so much for the price. Amazing. The broken trimmer attachment seems easily fixable. Only $16. I Highly Recommend this.</li>

    <li> So, this is going to sound a bit Negative-Nancy, and is loooong. But here goes:&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;In late May 2010, I purchased the T980. I was looking to replace my then nearly 10 year-old cheapo Norelco trimmer that had finally bit the dust. I went for the T980 because, well, I decided the beard was here to stay, so might as well invest in a \\&quot;higher quality\\&quot; trimmer. The T980 was Norelco&#x27;s initial \\&quot;vacuum\\&quot; trimmer (it has a little built in vacuum that&#x27;s supposed to suck in the hair as you trim). It was a bit big, and yes the \\&quot;turbo\\&quot; setting was loud, but for all intents and purposes, it worked well, and the vacuum feature was a nice touch (not perfect, but did greatly reduce the errant hairs all over the sink/tub). Less than a year and a half later, the adjustable beard trimmer attachment broke. Two of the plastic guides/teeth just snapped. I wasn&#x27;t doing anything out of the oridnary, and had never done anything to damage the unit or attachments. The teeth just snapped off mid-trim. Well, that was annoying, but I figured \\&quot;hey, no problem. I&#x27;ll just replace that one little part. Easy!\\&quot;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;After scouring the web for replacement parts with no luck, I contacted Norelco directly. They informed me that they no longer made my unit, as they had released version 2 of my model. Which didn&#x27;t have compatible parts. Furthermore, no other parts existed that would fit my trimmer. I figured surely they must have some older parts left, but was told no, no more parts for my model existed. So then I asked if I could get a refund or discounted price for the newer model. Nope!&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Begrudgingly, I decided to just buy another entire unit, but this time, go back to the cheapo model. Enter the G370.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;I have had the G370 almost exactly 1 year now with no complaints whatsoever...untie last weekend, when the exact same part broke. This time I went straight to Norelco. I knew they still made the G370. I knew they would have parts. After a 20min chat with one of their reps, he finally dug up the product code for the part I needed. Two problems though: 1) it actually wasn&#x27;t the right part - it was the hair trimmer attachment, I needed the beard trimmer; and 2) when I found the right part on my own, it cost almost $17...before tax and shipping!! While I am amazed to find that the G370 now costs over $50, I paid about $13 for it when I bought it a year ago. So there&#x27;s no way I&#x27;m paying ~$30 for a small, crappy, plastic replacement part. And, once again, I was informed no discount or refund of any kind would be provided.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;So, long story short: Norelco&#x27;s trimmers are great, but their attachments and customer service/loyalty are abhorrent. I am now off to buy my 3rd trimmer in as many years just because of a stupid, flimsy plastic part. Needless to say, I will NOT be buying Norelco. Ever. Had I paid what this unit is now selling for, I&#x27;d be even more furious. Buyer beware.e finally dug up the product code for the part I needed.     <li> I have waxed for years, but it is time-consuming to do at home and expensive at a salon (I&#x27;m also an esthetician, so I don&#x27;t like paying for it when I can do it myself- a pretty literal case of \\&quot;Who shaves the barber?\\&quot;). I looked at some of the pricier models that are especially for body grooming, but for $12.99, this seemed to be able to perform exactly the function I needed- to trim the hair without mangling the fancy china.  The biggest selling point for me was that the attachments, even the main trimmer attachment, can be removed and rinsed off.  I do not have the patience to be cleaning up little hairs with that teeny brush, so this feature scores major points with me.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Out of the Box:  I truly despise the plastic shrink-wrapping packing that is so ubiquitous these days, but I managed to open it without breaking into a full-on sweat. I appreciate the small, nylon bag that is provided to store the attachments, but it would be great if this came in box that could be used to organize and store it between uses.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;The plastic body is lightweight but sturdy and the seams are clean and smooth. For my purposes, the size and weight is perfect.  A rubberized coating would be an improvement on the buttons, as the on/off slides up and down and you need some grip, but there is a little notch that you can grab with your fingernail. The buttons are also shallow, so there is no threat of breaking them off.  The two comb attachments might be considered a bit on the flimsy side, but they should hold up fine because pressure is unnecessary while using them. The rest of the attachments feel very solid and theyall slide on and off and lock into place smoothly.  If you are using one of the comb attachments, it is easier to first slide it onto the trimmer attachment and adjust the height before you attach to the unit.  I tested all of the attachments except the beard/mustache comb, but I may try it next time, as the manual says that its lowest setting (1) is 2mm, compared to 4mm on the clipper attachment and I am looking to get the closest trim I can.  There are two charts showing the length of the settings in the manual [...].&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;I used the unit right from the box and it was surprisingly quiet. I used the clipper comb at setting 1 and mowed the lawn in seconds.  I did not have any tugging or pulling on the hair.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;I then tested the trimmer without the comb attachment and it worked well and trimmed down to a stubble. It&#x27;s very important to pull the skin taught and not put any pressure on it whatsoever. I can&#x27;t stress this enough because you will get nicks and cuts if you press down at all, especially in fleshier areas.  I wouldn&#x27;t recommend that anyone trim without the guard unless you are an experienced shaver and/or take a lot of care while doing so.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;I switched to the precision trimmer, which is a smaller version of the standard trimmer head and went in for some detail work.  Owwie Wowwie!  Totally my bad for going in so willy-nilly, but I found out the hard way that it is not only smaller in size, but the teeth are much shorter too. I will not be trying this again on the lower deck and I wouldn&#x27;t recommend it for anyone else either. Since it is so close and precise, it is a nice attachment for guys cleaning up their sideburns, goatees or more complicated facial hair.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;I don&#x27;t have any visible nose or ear hairs, but I tested the attachment anyway.  I put it into my nostril a few mms and swirled it around. I have no results to report.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Finally, I attached the mini-shaver and used it on the peach fuzz on my upper lip (of my face!) :)  I have fine, blonde hair and it is hardly noticeable, but the shaver did not remove the hair. I re-attached the trimmer and went over it first, then the shaver worked great.  The hair needs to be barely there and sticking straight up or it will not go into the tiny holes in the foil.  I used a small circular motion and the hair disappeared quickly.  I&#x27;m sure this would work well on the bikini area after a close trim, but it is so small that it would take forever- perfect for the face though.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Time spent: less than 15 minutes&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Total stars: 5 -I am sure there are better trimmers in existence, but the low price, the variety of attachments, and the convenience of cleaning make this a great product.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Total euphemisms for the vagina/pubic hair used in review- 7</li>

I use the detail trimmer to define the edges of my beard and the foil shaver to shave that down to nothing.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;They claim 35 minutes of battery and I believe them because I have not encountered an issue with run time. Because it uses NiMH batteries, it does require charging before use if it has been sitting for a while, maybe even a couple of weeks. Because it includes a very simple trickle charge, it should not be left on the charger constantly, or the batteries will wear out prematurely and run times will get unusably short. Unlike other similar shavers, the charger shuts off while the shaver is running, so it cannot be used like a typical plug-in charger. The batteries are also not replaceable. For these reasons, the shaver has a limited lifespan.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;I have mixed feelings about even giving 4 stars for the above reasons, but if you go into it thinking you&#x27;ll have it for a couple of years and toss it and that it costs only $25, I&#x27;d say it&#x27;s a good deal overall.</li>
